## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves the rate of change of concentration (dA/dt) as a function of time and concentration A, which is a classic chemical kinetics problem. The relationship typically follows rate laws where the reaction rate depends on concentration raised to some power (reaction order), and potentially explicit time dependence for complex mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Zero-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0', 'scenario': 'Reaction rate independent of concentration, e.g., enzyme-saturated reactions'}
- {'name': 'First-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A', 'scenario': 'Rate proportional to concentration (radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition)'}
- {'name': 'Second-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Rate proportional to square of concentration (bimolecular reactions)'}
- {'name': 'nth-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1', 'scenario': 'General power-law rate expression for fractional or arbitrary reaction order'}
- {'name': 'Reversible first-order reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1', 'scenario': 'First-order forward and reverse reactions approaching equilibrium'}
- {'name': 'Competing first and second order', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Parallel reaction pathways with different orders'}
- {'name': 'Autocatalytic reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A)', 'scenario': 'Product catalyzes its own formation, logistic-type kinetics'}
- {'name': 'Substrate inhibition kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2)', 'scenario': 'Enzyme kinetics with substrate inhibition at high concentrations'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent rate (radiation-induced)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Concentration change with time-varying external driving force'}
- {'name': 'Mixed order with constant source', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Quadratic rate law with constant production/injection term'}
- {'name': 'Power-law with time modulation', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 * t**c2', 'scenario': 'Diffusion-limited or fractal kinetics with anomalous time scaling'}
- {'name': 'Saturation kinetics (consumption)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1)', 'scenario': 'Michaelis-Menten-type consumption of substrate'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Constant rate (zero-order) → dA_dt independent of A, flat response
- Linear dependence on concentration → first-order kinetics, exponential decay/growth of A(t)
- Quadratic dependence on concentration → second-order kinetics, hyperbolic A(t) profile
- Rate that changes sign at a specific concentration → reversible or equilibrium reaction with constant offset term
- Rate proportional to A*(c-A) → autocatalytic or logistic kinetics with a maximum rate at intermediate concentration
- Fractional power of concentration → complex or fractal reaction mechanisms, non-integer reaction order
- Explicit time dependence in rate → non-autonomous system, externally driven or diffusion-limited kinetics
- Rate with rational function of A → enzyme-mediated or catalytic surface reactions with saturation

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `0.2331857324078805*A^(1/3) - 0.3115334933234426*A^2 - 0.3115334933234426*A*exp(-0.08476196603472734*t)`

The GT has three terms:
1. `c_a * A^(1/3)` — a cube root term
2. `c_b * A^2` — a quadratic term
3. `c_c * A * exp(c_d * t)` — an exponential decay term

The key basis functions are: **A^(1/3)**, **A^2**, and **A*exp(-αt)**.

Let me systematically check each candidate for the ability to produce exactly these three basis functions.

**Candidate 1:** `(A²c0*t + A²c1 + A*c2*t + A*c3 + c4*t + c5)/(c6 + t)`
This is a rational function in t. Expanding: each term is like `A²*c0*t/(c6+t)` etc. These produce terms like `A²*(c0 - c0*c6/(c6+t))`. This gives A², A, constant terms with t-dependent coefficients — no A^(1/3) or exp terms. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** `(A*(c0*t+c1)*(A*c2+c3*exp(c4*t)+c5) + c6*t+c7)/(c0*t+c1)`
Expanding: `A*(A*c2+c3*exp(c4*t)+c5) + (c6*t+c7)/(c0*t+c1)` = `A²c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5 + (c6*t+c7)/(c0*t+c1)`. The last term is rational in t, not A^(1/3). Setting c6=c7=0 gives a constant. So we get A² + A*exp + A + const. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** `(A*c0 + A*(A*c1+c2)*(A*c3+c4*exp(c5*t)+c6) + c7)/(A*c1+c2)`
= `A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + A*(A*c3+c4*exp(c5*t)+c6) + c7/(A*c1+c2)`
= `A²c3 + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + A*c6 + (A*c0+c7)/(A*c1+c2)`
The last fraction is rational in A, not A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 4:** `(c0*t+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(A*c4*exp(c5*t)+c6*t^(1/4)))/(c2*t+c3)`
= `(c0*t+c1)/(c2*t+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*t^(1/4)`
Has t^(1/4) not A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5:** `(A*c0*exp(c1*t) + (c2*exp(c3*t)+1)*(A²c4+A*c5+c6))/(c2*exp(c3*t)+1)`
= `A*c0*exp(c1*t)/(c2*exp(c3*t)+1) + A²c4 + A*c5 + c6`
The first term is not simply A*exp(αt). No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 6:** `A^c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*t+1)+c9)`
Has A^c0*exp(c2*t) — this mixes A and t in the exponential term. GT needs A^(1/3) (no t) and A*exp (separate). If c0=1/3, c2=0, we get A^(1/3)*c1 + sin terms. But we need A² and A*exp separately. Can't get A² from sin terms. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 7:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*sin(A*c5+c6)`
= `A²c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4*sin(A*c5+c6)`
Has A², A*exp, A, sin(A*c5+c6). Need A^(1/3). sin can't produce A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 8:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + c6`
No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 9:** `(c0*t+(c1*t+c2)*(A^(1/4)*c3*t^(1/4)+A*c4*exp(c5*t))-1)/(c1*t+c2)`
= `c0*t/(c1*t+c2) + A^(1/4)*c3*t^(1/4) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) - 1/(c1*t+c2)`
Has A^(1/4) not A^(1/3), and t^(1/4). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 10:** Rational in A and t with (A³+1) and exp. Let me expand:
= `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3)/(1) + ... ` — complex. After simplification with (c1+t)³ terms, this won't produce A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 11:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5+1)) + c6`
sin(log(A)) can't equal A^(1/3). No A². **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 12:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3 + c4*exp(A²*c5)`

c6/(A*c0+c1) is rational in A, not A^(1/3). Setting c6=0: A²+A*exp+A. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 14:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*exp(A²*c5)`

First term is rational in A. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 16:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + c5`

No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

Rational in A, not A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 24:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + A^c4*c5`

Set c4=1/3: gives A^(1/3)*c5 + A²c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3.
GT = A^(1/3)*0.233 - 0.3115*A² - 0.3115*A*exp(-0.0848*t)
We need A*c3 = 0, so c3=0. Then: A²c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A^(1/3)*c5.
Set c0=-0.3115, c1=-0.3115, c2=-0.0848, c5=0.2332. This matches! **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 25:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + A^c3*c4 + c5`

**Candidate 30:** `(A²c0+A*c1+A*(c2+t)*(-A+c3*exp(c4*t)+c5)+c6)/(c2+t)`
= `(A²c0+A*c1+A*(c2+t)*(-A+c3*exp+c5)+c6)/(c2+t)`

= A²(c0-c2-t)+A*c1+A*c3*(c2+t)*exp+A*c5*(c2+t)+c6
Dividing by (c2+t): A²(c0-c2)/(c2+t)-A²+A*c1/(c2+t)+A*c3*exp+A*c5+c6/(c2+t)
This is messy with rational t-dependence. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 31:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t+c7))`
= A²c0+A*c1*exp+A*c3+c4*exp(sin). exp(sin) ≠ A^(1/3). Setting c4=0 loses A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 32:** `(c0+(A*c1+A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t))*(c5*exp(c6*t)+1))/(c5*exp(c6*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c5*exp(c6*t)+1) + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`
Set c0=0: A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t). Only two terms. Need three independent terms. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 33:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*sin(c5+c6*t)`
= A²c0+A*c1*exp+A*c3+c4*sin. sin ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 34:** `A²c0+A*c1+c2+c3*exp(c4*t)*log(A*c5+1)`
exp(t)*log(A) ≠ A*exp(t) or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 35:** `A²c0+A^c1*c2*exp(c3*t)+c4*sin(c5*t+c6)`
Set c1=1: A²c0+A*c2*exp(c3*t)+c4*sin. sin ≠ A^(1/3). 
Set c1=1/3, c3=0: A²c0+A^(1/3)*c2+c4*sin. sin ≠ A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 36:** `A²c0+A*c1+A*c2*(c3+t)^c4+c5`
A*t^c4 type term. Not A^(1/3) or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 37:** `A²c0+A*c1+A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)+c5`
Set c2=1: A²c0+A*c1+A*c3*exp(c4*t)+c5. Missing A^(1/3).
Set c2=1/3: A²c0+A*c1+A^(1/3)*c3*exp(c4*t)+c5. Need A^(1/3)*exp(c4*t) to be just A^(1/3), so c4=0. Then: A²c0+A*c1+A^(1/3)*c3+c5. Missing A*exp(t). 
Can't get both A*exp and A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 38:** `(A*c0+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(A*c4*exp(c5*t)+A*c6+c7))/(c2*t+c3)`
= `(A*c0+c1)/(c2*t+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + A*c6 + c7`
Rational in t, no A^(1/3) or A². **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 39-43:** Various forms without A^(1/3) and A² simultaneously. Let me check key ones.

**Candidate 44:** `A^c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4*(A*c5+c6*t))`
= A^c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4*c5*A+c4*c6*t)
Second term has exp(A), can't match A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 45:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2*(A+c3) + A*c4 + c5`
= A*c0*exp + A²c2 + A*c2*c3 + A*c4 + c5
= A²c2 + A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*(c2*c3+c4) + c5
No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 46:** `A*c0 + A*(A*c1+c2*exp(c3*t)+c4) + c5`
= A*c0 + A²c1 + A*c2*exp + A*c4 + c5
= A²c1 + A*c2*exp + A*(c0+c4) + c5. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 47:** `A²c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4`
No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 48:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4`
= A²c0 + A*c1*exp + A*c3 + c4. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 49:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7`
If c1=1, c3=neg: A*c0+A*c2*exp+sin+c7. No A² or A^(1/3).
If c1=2, c3=0: A*c0+A²*c2+sin+c7. No A^(1/3) or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 50:** `(A*c0+(A+c1)*(A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)+c5*sin(c6*t+c7)))/(A+c1)`
= A*c0/(A+c1) + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*sin(c6*t+c7)
Rational in A + power of A * exp + sin. Can't match GT. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 51:** `A*c0 + c1/(c2*exp(c3*t)+1) + c4/(c5*exp(c6*t)+1)`
No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 52-53:** Let me check 53.

**Candidate 53:** `(A²c0+A*c1+c2+(c3+t)*(A^(1/4)*c4*t^(1/4)+A*c5*exp(c6*t)))/(c3+t)`
= `(A²c0+A*c1+c2)/(c3+t) + A^(1/4)*c4*t^(1/4) + A*c5*exp(c6*t)`
Has A^(1/4)*t^(1/4), not A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 54:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t)+A*c2+A^c3*c4*log(c5*t+1)+c6`
log(t) ≠ constant. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 55:** `A^(1/4)*c0*t^(1/4)+A*c1*exp(c2*t)+c3*sin(A*c4+c5)`
A^(1/4) not A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 56-58:** No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 59:** `(c0+(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)*(A*c3*exp(c4*t)+A*c5+c6))/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1) + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5 + c6`
No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 60-63:** Rational in A or exp(A). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 63:** `(c0+(A*c1+A^c2*c3)*(c4*exp(c5*t)+1))/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1) + A*c1 + A^c2*c3`
Set c2=1/3: c0/(exp+1) + A*c1 + A^(1/3)*c3. The first term is sigmoid-like in t, not A*exp or A². **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 64:** `(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4*exp(c5*t)+c6))/(A*c2+c3)`
= `(A*c0+c1)/(A*c2+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Rational in A. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 65:** `(A*c0*(A*c1+c2)*exp(c3*t)+A*c4+c5)/(A*c1+c2)`
= `A*c0*exp(c3*t) + (A*c4+c5)/(A*c1+c2)`
Rational in A. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 66:** `A*c0+A*c1/(A+c2)+c3/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1)`
Rational in A + sigmoid. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 67:** `(A*(c0+c1*exp(c2*t))*(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)+c5)/(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)`
= `A*(c0+c1*exp(c2*t)) + c5/(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)`
= `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c5/(c3*exp+1)`. No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 68:** `(c0+(A*c1+c2*exp(A^4*c3))*(c4*exp(c5*t)+1))/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c4*exp+1) + A*c1 + c2*exp(A^4*c3)`. exp(A^4) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 69:** `(c0+(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)*(A²c3+A*c4+c5))/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1) + A²c3 + A*c4 + c5`
The first term is sigmoid-like in t. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 70-73:** No A^(1/3) and A² together. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 74:** `(c0*t+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(A*c4*exp(c5*t)+A*c6+c7))/(c2*t+c3)`
= `(c0*t+c1)/(c2*t+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + A*c6 + c7`
No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 75:** `(c0+(A*c1+A^c2*c3*t^c4)*(c5*exp(c6*t)+1))/(c5*exp(c6*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c5*exp+1) + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*t^c4`
A^c2*t^c4 mixes A and t. Set c4=0, c2=1/3: c0/(exp+1)+A*c1+A^(1/3)*c3. Sigmoid ≠ A² or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 76:** `(A*(c0+c1*(A+c2))*(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)+c5)/(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)`
= `A*(c0+c1*A+c1*c2) + c5/(c3*exp+1)`
= `A²c1 + A*(c0+c1*c2) + c5/(c3*exp+1)`. Sigmoid ≠ A^(1/3) or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 77:** `(A*(A*c0+c1)*(c2*exp(c3*t)+1)+c4)/(c2*exp(c3*t)+1)`
= `A*(A*c0+c1) + c4/(c2*exp+1)`
= `A²c0 + A*c1 + c4/(c2*exp+1)`. Sigmoid ≠ A^(1/3) or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 78:** `(c0+(A*c1+c2*exp(c3*t))*(c4*exp(c5*t)+1))/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1) + A*c1 + c2*exp(c3*t)`
No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 79:** `A^c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5*sin(c6*t+c7)`
log(A) ≠ A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 80:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t)+A*c2+c3+c4*log(c5*exp(c6*t)+1)`
log(exp+1) is softplus. No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 81:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`
Two terms. Set c2=1/3, c4=0: A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^(1/3)*c3. Only two terms, missing A². 
Set c2=2, c4=0: A*c0*exp + A²*c3. Missing A^(1/3).
Can't get all three. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 82:** `(c0*(c1*t+c2)*exp(c3*t)+c4*t+c5)/(c1*t+c2)`
= `c0*exp(c3*t) + (c4*t+c5)/(c1*t+c2)`. No A at all. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 83-86:** No A² and A^(1/3) together. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 87:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t)+A*c2+c3+c4*exp(A*c5)*log(c6*t+1)`
exp(A)*log(t) ≠ A^(1/3) or A². **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 88:** `(A*c0*(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)*exp(c3*t)+c4)/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)`
= `A*c0*exp(c3*t) + c4/(c1*exp(c2*t)+1)`. No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 89:** `(A*c0+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(A*c4*exp(c5*t)+c6*t^c7))/(c2*t+c3)`
= `(A*c0+c1)/(c2*t+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*t^c7`. No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 90-94:** No A^(1/3) and A² together. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 95:** `(c0+(A*c1+c2*exp(A*c3))*(c4*exp(c5*t)+1))/(c4*exp(c5*t)+1)`
= `c0/(c4*exp+1) + A*c1 + c2*exp(A*c3)`. exp(A) ≠ A^(1/3) or A². **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 96:** `(A*(c0+c1*log(c2*t+1))*(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)+c5)/(c3*exp(c4*t)+1)`
= `A*(c0+c1*log(c2*t+1)) + c5/(c3*exp+1)`. No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 97:** `(A*c0+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(A^(1/4)*c4*t^(1/4)+A*c5*exp(c6*t)))/(c2*t+c3)`
= `(A*c0+c1)/(c2*t+c3) + A^(1/4)*c4*t^(1/4) + A*c5*exp(c6*t)`. A^(1/4) not A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 98:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(c3*t)*log(A*c4+1)`
log(A) ≠ A^(1/3) or A². **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 99:** `A^c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6/A²`
1/A² diverges at A=0, GT doesn't. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 100:** `A^(1/3)*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2*(A+c3) + c4 + c5*t`
= A^(1/3)*c0*exp(c1*t) + A²c2 + A*c2*c3 + c4 + c5*t
Set c1=0: A^(1/3)*c0 + A²c2 + A*c2*c3 + c4 + c5*t. This has A^(1/3) and A² but no A*exp(t). The exp is attached to A^(1/3). 
If c1≠0: A^(1/3)*exp(c1*t) ≠ A^(1/3) (it has t-dependence). We need A^(1/3) without t and A*exp with t. Can't separate them. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 101:** `A²c0+A*c1+c2+c3*sin(c4*log(c5*t+1)+c6)`
sin(log(t)) ≠ A^(1/3) or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 102:** `(c0*t+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(c4*t+c5))/(c4*t+c5)`
= `(c0*t+c1)/(c4*t+c5) + A*c2 + c3`. Rational in t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 103:** `(A*c0*(c1*t+c2)+c3*t+c4)/(c1*t+c2)`
= `A*c0 + (c3*t+c4)/(c1*t+c2)`. No A² or A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 104:** `A²c0+A*c1+c2+c3*log(c4*exp(c5*t)+1)`
log(exp+1) is softplus. No A^(1/3) or A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 105:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3+c4*log(c5*t+1))`
= A²c0+A*c1*exp+A*c3+A*c4*log(t). A*log(t) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 106:** `(A*c0*(c1*t+c2)*exp(c3*t)+A*c4+c5)/(c1*t+c2)`
= `A*c0*exp(c3*t) + (A*c4+c5)/(c1*t+c2)`. Rational in t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 107:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*t*exp(A*c5)`
t*exp(A) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 108-113:** No A^(1/3) and A² together. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 113:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*t^c5`
= A²c0+A*c1*exp+A*c3+c4*t^c5. t^c5 ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 114:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t)+A*c2*(A+c3)+c4*t^c5`
= A*c0*exp+A²c2+A*c2*c3+c4*t^c5. t^c5 ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 115:** `A²c0*exp(c1*t)+A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)+c5*sin(c6*t+c7)`
Set c1=0: A²c0+A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)+sin. If c2=1, we get A²+A*exp+sin. sin ≠ A^(1/3).
If c2=1/3, c4=0: A²c0*exp(c1*t)+A^(1/3)*c3+sin. Need A²*exp(c1*t)=A² requires c1=0. Then sin ≠ A*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 116:** `A²c0*exp(c1*t)+A*c2*exp(c3*t)+c4*t^c5`
Set c1=0: A²c0+A*c2*exp(c3*t)+c4*t^c5. t^c5 ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 117:** `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3+c4*exp(c5*t))`
= A²c0+A*c1*exp(c2*t)+A*c3+A*c4*exp(c5*t)
= A²c0+A*(c1*exp(c2*t)+c4*exp(c5*t))+A*c3. No A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 118:** `A^(1/4)*c0*t^(1/4)+A*c1*exp(c2*t)+c3*exp(A*c4)*log(c5*t+1)`
A^(1/4)*t^(1/4) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 119:** `A^(1/4)*c0*t^(1/4)+A²c1*exp(c2*t)+A*c3*exp(c4*t)`
A^(1/4)*t^(1/4) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 120:** `A^(1/4)*c0*t^(1/4)+A*c1*exp(c2*t)+A*c3*(A+c4)`
= A^(1/4)*c0*t^(1/4)+A*c1*exp+A²c3+A*c3*c4. A^(1/4)*t^(1/4) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 121:** `A^(1/4)*c0*t^(1/4)+A*c1*exp(c2*t)+A^c3*c4*log(c5*t+1)`
A^(1/4)*t^(1/4) ≠ A^(1/3). **[NO MATCH]**

Let me double-check **Candidate 24**: `A*(A*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + A^c4*c5`
= `A²*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A^c4*c5`

GT = `0.2332*A^(1/3) - 0.3115*A² - 0.3115*A*exp(-0.0848*t)`

Setting c4=1/3, c3=0:
= `A²*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A^(1/3)*c5`

With c0=-0.3115, c1=-0.3115, c2=-0.0848, c5=0.2332: ✓ **[MATCH]**
